### Audit тАФ March 30, 2026 13:10 CET (ACCOUNTING CORRECTION)

**Errors found and corrected:**

#### Error 1: Day 43 balance understated
- LEDGER reported тВм3,768.05 excluding 4GLD (тВм475.03)
- Actual Day 43 balance: **тВм4,243.08**
- The Day 44 LEDGER showed "+тВм474 (internal reclassification)" as if it were an adjustment тАФ in reality it was a previous accounting error

#### Error 2: XEON entry price incorrect
- When adding XEON to the valuation script, тВм148.40 was used as entry price instead of тВм140.50 (actual purchase price)
- This generated inflated units and inflated value
- Corrected: 14.788 units at actual price тВм140.50, but the XEON book value is тВм476.91 (what remains after funding DXS3 and NATO)

#### Error 3: DXS3 entry price incorrect in LEDGER
- Day 44 trades were recorded at тВм29.50/unit (incorrect price)
- Actual DXS3 market price: ~тВм5.69/unit
- Total invested in DXS3 remains correct (тВм1,200)
